Please try again   </div></div></div> </span>    </div>            <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R35MDIQC5Z9BGE" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">12 of 13 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R35MDIQC5Z9BGE/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/181-1038543-7025645?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00IF4NGEU&nodeID=541966&store=pc"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R35MDIQC5Z9BGE/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/181-1038543-7025645?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00IF4NGEU&nodeID=541966&store=pc"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">One of the BEST SSDs You Can Buy Today</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A6Z212SNV77EH/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/181-1038543-7025645" class="noTextDecoration">Boba's Daddy Figure</a>   </span> <span class="a-color-secondary"> on September 30, 2014</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R35MDIQC5Z9BGE" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Style Name: Reseller Kit<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Size Name: 480GB<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   This is one fast and highly reliable SSD. You can compare specs till your face turns orange, at which time you may buy a Samsung or other aggressively spec'd out product.  Remember that THIS Intel 730 is not only super fast (though it won't finish #1 in any group of tests), it's super reliable in case of a drastic computer failure.  Because it uses big capacitors that keep voltage up even when power is suddenly removed, it will complete its writes and not create broken files, as will happen on blazing Samsung/etc drives.  The Micron based Crucial drives are the other brand that offers good speed plus solid reliability.  This Intel is intended for top of the line performance in a DESKTOP or server chassis environment.  Don't even consider it for your laptop, as the heat and extra current usage is not appropriate for laptop usage.  The aluminum case dissipates heat well.  Over a few years I've installed several 530 and 730 models, and they ALL RUN FLAWLESSLY and still report as &#34;100% good condition&#34; with SSD test softwares.  A highly recommended product for PCs running versions of Windows.  Be sure to use a secondary drive for user data/documents storage and for &#34;scratch&#34; drive locations and temp files, as on all desktop SSD installations, to keep your users very happy. </div> What's not to love?</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A2CPTH3C7XTHPM/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/181-1038543-7025645" class="noTextDecoration">ViolentMetaphor</a>   </span> <span class="a-color-secondary"> on June 11, 2014</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R1E0CUEYW786D8" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Style Name: Reseller Kit<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Size Name: 240GB<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   Intel has a good reputation as an SSD manufacturer.  Even if they don't directly manufacture the device, they have high standards that some of the other vendors don't match.<br><br>This SSD has a capacitor for preventing corruption from power loss.  A surprisingly low number of SSDs have a capacitor to avoid corruption.<br><br>These are expensive but there are few non-enterprise SSDs that have capacitors.  If I had to do it over again, I would check out the new Crucial SSDs which are significantly cheaper and also have a capacitor.  Either way, I wouldn't regret buying these again since Intel has a great reputation in this area.<br><br>I have read that they run hot.  My case (Fractal Design Define R4) has a 140mm fan right in front of them.  I wouldn't necessarily recommend a R4 (or Fractal Design) but a case with a fan in front of the drives may help. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="0"
